    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function(){

            // Main banner hiding function

            $.promotionalBanner({
                originalContentId: '#promotional--cont',
                replacementContentId: '',
                expiryDateTime: '2017-09-07T23:59:59',
            });

            // Countdown functions

            var oneDay = 24*60*60*1000;
            var currentDate = new Date();
            var endDate = new Date(2016,3,7,11,59);
            var diffDays = Math.round(Math.abs((currentDate.getTime() - endDate.getTime())/(oneDay)));
            var dateText = '';
            if(diffDays == 0){
                            dateText = 'today';
            } else if(diffDays == 1){
                            dateText = 'in ' + diffDays + ' day';
            } else {
                            dateText = 'in ' + diffDays + ' days';
            }

            $('#countdown').text(dateText);

            console.log(currentDate);
            console.log(endDate);
            console.log(diffDays);

        });
        </script>

    var brands = ['lodges', 'holiday-parks', 'boat-holidays', 'cottages', 'holiday-parks-in-europe', 'city-breaks'];
    function navToggle() {
        if ($('.sliding-menu-wrapper input[type="checkbox"]').is(':checked')) {
            $('.mobile-scrolling').scrollTop(0);
            $('.mobile-nav').addClass('active');
            if ($('.sliding-menu-wrapper.slide-left input[type="checkbox"]').is(':checked')){
                $('#nav-icon').addClass('open');
            }
            //$('body').on('touchmove', false);
            $('body').addClass('lock-screen');
        } else {
            $('#nav-icon').removeClass('open');
            $('.mobile-nav').removeClass('active');
            $('body').removeClass('lock-screen');
             // $('body').off('touchmove', false);
        }
    }
    function lastMinuteDeals() {
        $.each(brands, function(i,v) {
            var d = new Date();
            var curr_date = d.getDate();
            var curr_month = d.getMonth() + 1;
            var curr_year = d.getFullYear();
            var startdate = curr_date + "-" + curr_month + "-" + curr_year;
            if (v == "boat-holidays" || v == "cottages"){
                d.setDate(d.getDate() + 3);
                curr_date = d.getDate();
                curr_month = d.getMonth() + 1;
                curr_year = d.getFullYear();
                startdate = curr_date + "-" + curr_month + "-" + curr_year;
            }
             
            $("#" + v + "-last-minute-deals, #" + v + "-lmd-link").attr("href", "/" + v + "/all-regions?adult=2&child=0&infant=0&nights=4&range=7&pets=0&start=" + startdate + "&sortorder=4");
        });
    }
    //Roundal href...
    function activeStateDeals() {
        if (_websiteRoute) {
            var active_nav_route = _websiteRoute.split('/')[0];

                $('#main-nav-' + active_nav_route).addClass('active');

                    curr_month = d.getMonth() + 1,

                    d.setDate(d.getDate() + 3);
                    curr_date = d.getDate();
                    curr_month = d.getMonth() + 1;
                    curr_year = d.getFullYear();
                    startdate = curr_date + "-" + curr_month + "-" + curr_year;
                }

    function msieversion() {
        var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
        var msie = ua.indexOf("MSIE ");
        if (msie > 0 || !!navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident.*rv\:11\./) || navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf('firefox') > -1) {
            $('.main-nav').height(101);
        }
        return false;
    }
    document.onclick = function (evt) {
        var tgt = (evt && evt.target) || event.srcElement,
            scr = document.body.scrollTop;
 
        if (tgt.tagName == "A" && tgt.href.slice(-1) == "#") {
            window.location.href = "#";
            document.body.scrollTop = scr;
            return false;
        }
    }
    ;(function( $, window, document, undefined )
    {
        $.fn.doubleTapToGo = function( params )
        {
            if( !( 'ontouchstart' in window ) &&
                !navigator.msMaxTouchPoints &&
                !navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().match( /windows phone os 7/i ) ) return false;
 
            this.each( function()
            {
                var curItem = false;
 
                $( this ).on( 'click', function( e )
                {
                    var item = $( this );
                    if( item[ 0 ] != curItem[ 0 ] )
                    {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        curItem = item;
                    }
                });
 
                $( document ).on( 'click touchstart MSPointerDown', function( e )
                {
                    var resetItem = true,
                        parents   = $( e.target ).parents();
 
                    for( var i = 0; i < parents.length; i++ )
                        if( parents[ i ] == curItem[ 0 ] )
                            resetItem = false;
 
                    if( resetItem )
                        curItem = false;
                });
            });
            return this;
        };
    })( jQuery, window, document );

	<script>
ga('require', 'ec');
function gaAddPromo (promoFieldObject) {
    try {
        ga('ec:addPromo', promoFieldObject);
    } catch(err) {}
}
function buildPromoFieldObject (sel, attr) {
    var obj = {};
    try {
        obj = JSON.parse($(sel).attr(attr));
    } catch(err){}
    return obj;
}
function gaSendPromoClick (promoFieldObject) {
    try {
        ga('ec:setAction', 'promo_click');
        ga('send', 'event', 'Internal Promotions', 'click', promoFieldObject.name);
    } catch(err){}
}
